US, Russia, and Japan Expand Air Forces; Britain Prepares to Catch Up Quickly 72

Minister of Aviation's Strong Air Force Policy Advances Rapidly in Both Houses of Parliament

(London) British Aviation Minister Marquess Londonderry declared in the House of Lords today that Britain must build a strong air force that is no less than other countries in the world. Britain's air force strength has now fallen to fifth place, and he wants to catch up quickly. The current weakness of the air force cannot be tolerated for long. We must make these islands and the British Empire safe in the skies. He also said that he deeply regretted that other countries had failed to reduce their air forces to the level of Britain, so he will do his best to avoid competition in the sky arms race. In the future, while Britain expands its air force, it will continue to work to persuade other countries to reduce their sky arms to the same level as Britain. However, he also reminded the parliamentarians that the United States, Russia, and Japan are currently expanding their air forces, and their strength will be unprecedented, so he has doubts about whether the continued efforts to reduce sky arms will be successful. The British Air Ministry's preparations for expanding the air force will advance rapidly in both houses. After Lord Lloyd and the Duke of Sutherland made requests in the House of Lords, citing the Aviation Minister's proposal, Admiral Sutter also introduced a bill in the House of Commons, strongly stating the fear and unease about the weakness of the British air force. When Sutter mentioned that the British air force had fallen to fifth place, the parliamentarians responded with cries of "shameful" and "shameful," which also shows the attitude of the parliamentarians. (National Telegram, 30th)

Comparison of World Air Forces 73

Britain Wants to Restore Its Status as the Number One Air Force Power; Air Routes to Be Extended to Hong Kong

(London) As a result of today's debate in the House of Commons on Britain's sky defenses, a motion by Conservative Party Member Admiral Sutter to draw attention to the weakness of Britain's air defenses was unanimously rejected. It was followed by a vote of 151 to 31 to adopt a motion by Conservative Party Member James supporting the British government's policies listed in the British Disarmament Draft Treaty. Lord President Baldwin, in closing the debate, said that Great Britain's position regarding its air, sea, and land defenses today cannot be isolated from the world. The disarmament situation is extremely complex, but no one in the government is disappointed. They are still working hard to reach a compromise in various ways. At the same time, the House of Lords also discussed the same issue. Aviation Minister Marquess Londonderry claimed that Britain was the number one air force power after the European War, but it has now fallen to fifth place.

France currently has 1,650 military aircraft, Russia 1,300 to 1,500, the United States 1,000 to 1,100, Italy 1,000, and Britain only 700. Britain must abandon its unilateral disarmament policy. If reductions can never achieve equality among countries, then Britain has no choice but to build more. At the same time, it will continue to work to seek international compromises and establish the lowest possible equal rate so that other countries can join.

During the debate in the House of Commons, Under-Secretary of State for Air Sassoon replied to a question from Conservative Party Member Balfour, saying that he did not want to increase the status of the British Air Force Commander in the Far East at present. He also said that the possibility of extending British air routes to Hong Kong is currently being actively considered. (Reuters dispatch, 29th)

Intensified Trade War Between Britain and Japan; British Parliament Debates Abolishing the British-Japanese Commercial Treaty 74

Parliament Unanimous in Opposing Japanese Goods; Government Favors Concerted Action with Various Countries

(London) Conservative Party Member Fowler moved in the House of Commons today, demanding the abolition of the British-Japanese Commercial Treaty and the use of tariffs or prohibitions to restrict the competition of Japanese goods within the British Empire. Fowler asked the government to explain its intentions in the event that it could not reach a satisfactory quota agreement with Japan, and asked the government to immediately find a way to alleviate the competition of Japanese imported goods in the British territory and the British Empire market. If necessary, it could abandon contracts that hindered effective action. Fowler criticized the government for not taking concrete action and praised India's vigor in dealing with this issue. Fowler also said that the unfair trade situation between Britain and Japan is recognized by the Japanese themselves. Japan demands that any agreement be limited to Britain, Palestine, Ceylon, East Fiji, and the Straits Settlements. Britain cannot accept this as a basis for discussion.

Conservative Party Member Proctor seconded, saying that the government should send a cotton industry commissioner and organize a committee of experts to study methods of improving the cotton industry. He believed that they could create a plan for Lancashire to use Indian cotton, so as to eliminate Japan's request to share the benefits of the Indian market and eliminate the tools Japan holds in negotiations.

Conservative Party Member Holmesley said that Japan's current industrial policy cannot coexist with the economic security of the British Empire. In his opinion, the British-Japanese Commercial Treaty will have to be abolished sooner or later. He argued that the government should abolish this treaty under normal circumstances and not wait and see, which would make it difficult to clean up. Lancashire has decided to use more Indian cotton, which is not just lip service from Lancashire.

Minister of Commerce Runciman replied that if the government immediately abolished the British-Japanese Commercial Treaty, he did not see how Lancashire could gain much benefit. The government would rather exhaust other methods before taking this final step. Britain and Western countries are all feeling great difficulties with Japan. Countries may have to take concerted action in this major economic event. Therefore, Britain is now advising Japan that it is better to be on friendly terms with Britain than to pursue a policy of competition that causes resentment. He hopes that this problem can ultimately be resolved with wisdom and strategy.

This debate showed the consensus of the parliament, and Fowler's motion was unanimously supported. (Reuters dispatch, 29th)

(Tokyo) According to the Eastern News, the British House of Commons discussed the issue of preventing Japanese goods from entering the country yesterday. The proposal by Lancashire elected Member Weiying was explained by the British Minister of Commerce and passed the House of Commons by a majority. It also said that the Netherlands has also decided to cooperate with the British cotton industry to boycott Japanese goods and plans to hold a joint Anglo-Dutch cotton industry conference in The Hague on December 2 to discuss this matter. (United News dispatch, 30th)

The test results were satisfactory. Sassoon also replied to a question from Conservative Party Member Buster, saying that the possibility of extending British air routes to Hong Kong is currently being actively considered. (Reuters dispatch, 29th)

Rome Considers the Timing Unripe for the Convocation of the Seven-Power Conference 75

Avenol to Lobby in England; Secret Negotiations Between France and Germany Underway

Rome Foreign newspapers have recently spread rumors that Italian Prime Minister Mussolini is attempting to unite the seven major powers to maintain world peace and stability. The authorities here believe that there is no basis for this, as Mussolini, although he agrees to the reorganization of the League of Nations so that the United States, Russia, Germany, and Japan can all join, his motive has not reached the appropriate time, so it is difficult to achieve successful results. (National Telegram, 29th)

Rome Foreign countries spread two important news items: (1) Prime Minister Mussolini recently met with the British Ambassador to Italy, Sir Drummond, and discussed various German proposals, as well as Germany's attitude towards the Danzig Corridor if it makes a request. Representatives of the four-power treaty signatories should be convened to discuss it. (2) The convening of a seven-nation conference, especially inviting Russia to participate, will soon be realized. Recently, responsible parties denied both news items, saying that they were completely unfounded. (Havas dispatch, 29th)

(Geneva) Some parties are spreading several impactful news items about the League of Nations Secretary-General's trip to Rome to shake people's hearts. The Havas reporter recently received reliable information that Avenol's trip to Rome was due to the death of Shereca, the former Italian representative to the League of Nations Executive Council, and he had to go to pay his respects and visit Prime Minister Mussolini. However, when Avenol met with Mussolini, the Italian authorities did not mention Italy's intention to withdraw from the League of Nations, nor did they advocate amending the League of Nations organization. What Mussolini is most concerned about is the future of the disarmament conference. The Italian authorities are eager for it to succeed and want to use the League of Nations mechanism to promote it. Only when it is ineffective or dangerous will consultations be held outside the League of Nations. Avenol, at the invitation of British parliamentarians, will go to England to give two speeches explaining the organization of the League of Nations. After visiting England, Avenol will continue to visit other European capitals, as it is his duty as Secretary-General of the League of Nations. (Havas dispatch, 29th)

Japan Expresses Unwillingness to Be Persuaded 76

(Tokyo) Regarding the proposal by Italian Prime Minister Mussolini to reorganize the League of Nations and persuade the United States, Japan, and Russia to join the Four-Power Agreement, the Japanese Foreign Ministry expressed its sympathy for Prime Minister Mussolini's actions from the perspective that restoring the disarmament cause and European peace are prerequisites. However, it is negative about the plan to persuade Japan to join the European peace issue, because Japan is willing to cooperate in the disarmament cause, but in order to proceed, European countries must first make efforts to rebuild peace. Japan has not yet seen the results, so it cannot rashly participate in the seven-nation conference. (Dentsu dispatch, 30th)

Belgian Prime Minister Calls for Reopening Disarmament; 77

The Treaty of Locarno Cannot Be Unilaterally Abolished; Parliamentarians Demand Strict Consolidation of National Defense

Brussels Belgian Foreign Minister Hymans today called on countries to continue the disarmament conference and closer international cooperation, stating that Belgium intends to maintain its obligations to the Treaty of Locarno and the League of Nations with Britain and France. The Treaty of Locarno will not be damaged in the slightest by Germany's withdrawal from the League of Nations. The treaty cannot be unilaterally denied. Belgium does not object to discussions between the powers, but asks that events directly related to Belgium's interests not be discussed when Belgian representatives are not present. (Reuters dispatch, 29th)

Brussels Foreign Minister Hymans made a statement to the Chamber of Deputies, saying that Germany's sudden withdrawal from the League of Nations and the disarmament conference is certainly worrying, but we should remain calm in dealing with the situation. In addition to this, there are factors in the international situation that should be reassuring, such as the treaties signed between the Soviet Union and its Western neighbors, the non-aggression treaty to be signed between Germany and Poland, the friendship between France and Britain, and the rapprochement between France and Italy. Belgium will do its utmost with Britain and France to protect the various international cooperation mechanisms. Hymans concluded that the Rhineland Agreement in the Treaty of Locarno, which guarantees Belgium's borders, cannot be changed. The audience applauded upon hearing this. The Chamber continued to discuss foreign policy, with a speech by Socialist leader Vandervelde, who first explained the fact that Germany is rearming, saying that he therefore agrees with Foreign Minister Hymans's views on the League of Nations and the disarmament conference. Aggressors should be prevented, but Vandervelde believes that all countries should disarm in unison. In his view, if all countries disarm in unison, Germany will be forced by the general trend to agree to disarmament. Vandervelde Shi said that the private conversations between countries are harmful to international public opinion, and said that only France is resolutely maintaining peace and seeking the realization of disarmament, but France is prepared to talk to Hitler alone, which may be a mistake. Catholic Party Member Sinzo criticized Hymans for his political and economic failures and demanded strict consolidation of national defense. He concluded that the Belgian people believe that Belgium should strictly guard its borders. (Havas dispatch, 29th)

(Berlin) Although the German side is keeping the secret negotiations between France and Germany in Berlin strictly confidential, German newspapers often transcribe foreign news about the issue but do not comment on it. The Little Entente United; Striving to Join Hands with Soviet Russia 79

Czechoslovakia and Other Countries Prepare to Formally Recognize Russia; French Influence in the Balkans Reduced; Pan-European Conference to Be Convened in Vienna Tomorrow to Organize Five Major Groups to Restructure the Economy

(Berlin) The midday newspaper Moscow correspondent obtained semi-official news that Czechoslovakia or the entire Little Entente will recognize Soviet Russia, which is expected to happen soon. The various events that have recently occurred in Turkey, Romania, Bulgaria, Greece, Yugoslavia, and Czechoslovakia, as well as the several conventions signed between these countries, have led observers to expect that Central and Eastern European countries will form a large peace group and be linked to Soviet Russia. If this move becomes a reality, one of the results will be a reduction in French influence in the Balkans, and the hegemony of the French in Geneva will be greatly reduced because they will no longer have the support of these small countries. As for Soviet Russia, although it has no direct relationship with the future Balkan alliance, it seems that the support of the Russians is indispensable if the Balkan states want to create a united front to the West. Judging from the recent remarks of the Romanian Foreign Minister in the Turkish capital, it can be seen that the Balkan states all want to obtain the support of Soviet Russia, and there is no doubt that Russia is willing to be the supporter of small countries. (National Telegram, 30th)

Vienna Count Coudenhove-Kalergi, Chairman of the Pan-European Union, gave a speech at a press conference here today, explaining the purpose of the Pan-European Economic Conference, which is to stop the world economic panic. The conference is scheduled to open in Vienna on the second of next month and is convened by the Pan-European Union. Kalergi also said that the problems that need to be solved at present are, first, the currency crisis, and second, the restructuring of the European economy based on local agreements to create the following five economic groups: (1) the Danube River countries, (2) the Balkan Peninsula countries, (3) the Scandinavian Peninsula countries, (4) the Baltic Sea coastal countries, and (5) the Soviet Union. If Europe wants to fight effectively with the Americas and the East, it must establish economic groups. As for the League of Nations in its current form, it can be said to be on its last legs. We must find a way to make it survive, and the way is to reform the League of Nations with the federal system as a new foundation, so that it will no longer be a union of several countries, but a union of several groups of countries, namely (1) the Far East, (2) the Soviet Union, (3) the Pan-American Union, (4) the British Empire, and (5) the United States of Europe. US War Debts Owed by Various Countries About to Expire Again 88

Britain, Italy, and Other Countries Promise to Repay Part of the Debt; France, Belgium, and Poland Have Made No Indication

(Washington) The US State Department is processing negotiations to collect $153,001,387 in war debts due in mid-December. It is expected that Italy will be the first to reach an agreement. Italy owes a total of about $2,000,000,000 in war debts and should pay $2,223,905 this time. It is expected to pay $1,000,000. In addition, Czechoslovakia, Romania, Lithuania, Estonia, and Yugoslavia are also negotiating with the US government to modify or pay part of the debt. Czechoslovakia owes a total of $312,811,433 in US war debts and has repaid $19,804,178 without default. It is now requesting to modify the debt to obtain some concessions. Rome The interest payment period for the $100 million Morgan loan borrowed by Italy is now due. Although the loan contract states "gold bullion," the Italian government has decided to pay in US dollar paper currency. (Reuters dispatch, 29th)

Five Routes of Sichuan Army Suppress Bandits 89

Yilong and Peng'an armies agreed to join forces. Chiang instructed Liu Xiang to launch a new strategy of suppression.

Hankou Correspondence: Since Liu Xiang ordered a general offensive of the Sichuan bandit suppression army, Chairman Chiang again sent a stern telegram urging them to fight and not to stand by and watch any longer. In recent days, the battles on all fronts have made considerable progress. The armies were originally divided into six routes, with Deng Xihou, Tian Songyao, Li Qixiang, Yang Sen, Wang Lingji, and Liu Cunhou serving as commanders-in-chief. Liu was dismissed for the loss of Sui and Xuan. The sixth route was then taken over by Fan Shaozeng, but Fan was originally under the fifth route and did not establish a separate banner. The battle locations were along the Qu River and the Jialing River. The Qu River line was divided into left and right routes, with Yang Sen and Li Qixiang in charge of the left route, and Wang Lingji and Fan Shaozeng in charge of the right route. On the 23rd, Yang's troops, Luo Jiede, Xia Jiong, Yang Hancheng, Gao Dezhou, and other four brigades, recaptured Yingshan County. The puppet army commander He Wei was wounded in the waist and died in battle. One puppet division commander and two regiment commanders were killed. The remaining bandits fled in disarray towards Jiangkou and Sanhui. Yang's troops then crossed Yingcheng and advanced northward. The third route, Li Qixiang's troops, also cheered and marched out, taking advantage of Yang's victory. Luo's division and Wang's brigade have advanced to the Wangjiachang line in Peng'an, and Li's troops have advanced to Dumulin in Yingxi, and Li Zongfang's brigade has advanced to Fengdengpu in Yingxi North, connecting with Yang's troops and launching a suppression campaign towards Jiangkou and Peng'an. Some of the bandits who fled from Yingshan fled to Jiangkou, and some fled to Sanhui. At that time, Sanhui had been recovered by the Fifth Route Army, so they joined forces with the bandits who were originally based in Sanhui and launched a large-scale counterattack. Taipingyan, Leiyinpu, Liangjiaoyan, Panshichang, Yujiasi and other places were frequently attacked by the main force of the bandits. After the Fifth Route Army fought back, the bandits were unable to succeed. However, the progress of this route was also slightly delayed due to its being contained. The Second Route Army, Tian Songyao's troops, and the First Route Army, Deng Xihou's troops, were jointly responsible for the Jialing River line. They originally planned to hold the left bank firmly and then launch a joint suppression campaign after Deng's army was concentrated. When the bandits came to attack, they sent Li Weiruyi and other troops to cross the Jialing River forcibly. After several days of fierce fighting, it was reported that they had occupied Tudie, Xiaojiashan, Pingtougai, LijiaShan, Shangyuanguan, Lujiagou and other places, advancing more than eighty li along the entire line. Part of Deng's troops has arrived at Zhaoguang, and all of them can be concentrated within a few days and join the battle group. The plan for five routes to encircle and suppress the bandits has been completed in the first step. The bandit suppression armies of each route are now proposing the slogan of joining forces at Peng'an and Yilong, connecting Qu and Jia into one line, and at the same time recovering Sui and Xuan to destroy the bandit's nest. According to a telegram from the Sichuan Bandit Suppression Headquarters, the main force of the bandits is still in Sui and Xuan, and they will invade from time to time. When Sui and Xuan are recovered in the future, a bloody battle will be unavoidable. Liu Xiang previously sent his representative in Hankou, Qiu Jia, to Gan to meet with Chiang, report on the bandit situation, and ask for instructions. After Chiang personally instructed him on the new strategy, he ordered him to convey it to Liu and implement it accordingly. Qiu completed his mission in Gan and returned to Hankou on the 25th, and has telegraphed all the points instructed by Chairman Chiang to Liu Xiang for a reply. (28th)

Uprising of the Militia in Deng County 90

Thousands gathered for fierce fighting for more than twenty days. Liu Zhi sent the head of the security department to investigate.

Kaifeng Correspondence: Deng County is adjacent to Hubei and is located in the remote southwest corner of Henan Province. Since the beginning of the Republic of China, it has formed a situation where the sky is high and the emperor is far away, and strength is king. All the power of life and death is in the hands of the leaders of the Republic of China, and these local emperors often fight each other due to conflicts of interest. Once a dispute arises, it lasts for several months. Moreover, in order to compete for existence, they all collude with and incorporate bandits to expand their personal power. Within the territory, from Sunzhuang in the east to Tangshan, Yushan, and Hengshan in the west, and from Menglou and Weijialou, which are adjacent to Hubei, in the south, sixty li from east to west and fifty li from north to south, there are no people due to banditry. More than 8,000 hectares of fertile land have become grass that is six or seven feet deep, and foxes and rabbits have become dens. All of this was created by these people. Recently, Tian Ziyue's troops in the third district and Dai Huanzhang's troops in the fifth district started a riot, and it has not been resolved for two months. Liu Zhi has sent Feng Jianfei, the head of the security department, to investigate and order both sides to stop fighting and wait for a political solution. However, it is not yet possible to predict whether it will be effective. Deng County is divided into nine districts, and each district commander has 500 to 600 regular soldiers, up to 1,500 to 1,600. Conflicts often arise between them. In the 20th year of the Republic of China, Yang Jiesan, who was sent by Bie Tingfang, the commander of the bandit suppression in Wanxi, oppressed them too much, and they once united to oppose Yang. Later, they elected Zheng Xiangzhou as the director of the nine district offices and the deputy director of the Dengnei-Zhe (Xichuan) joint defense office. The districts were at peace for more than a year. However, Zheng was extremely weak, and last winter he was unable to withstand the pressure from the districts and left in anger. This year, Bie Tingfang was appointed as the commander of the Nanyang guerrilla, and sent Zhao Zesan as the captain of the Deng County Militia Detachment. Zhao and Sun Xianzhou, Sun Wenshan, and Pi Wenxuan were known to be friendly, and people called them the pro-Neixiang faction, while Dai Huanzhang and Zhang Zhenjiang were originally bandits who were recruited and stationed at Wenquji, about ten li northwest of the city, with more than a thousand men, and the fighting force was the strongest. Guo Jingting, Ding Jiayi, and others were incompatible with Zhao Zesan, and people called them the anti-Neixiang faction. The third district is in the east of the city, and the fifth district is in the south of the city. The two districts are adjacent to each other. Tian and Dai had long had a grudge. In the 20th year of the Republic of China, they fought fiercely for several months, and both sides were exhausted before they stopped fighting. At the end of September, Lou, a villager from Jinglou Village, which originally belonged to Tian Ziyue's jurisdiction in the third district, was close to Dai and seized several villages to break away from Tian's shackles and return to Dai. Before the incident was reported, Tian knew about it and led a team to surround his house. Only three of the twelve family members escaped. Then Dai united Zhang Zhenjiang and Guo Jingting to help Lou, and in Lou's name, secretly attacked Tian's camp and Tian's house (Tian's district headquarters was located in Jitan Town), killing his mother, younger brother, and others. After the incident, Wang Youqiao, the administrative inspector of the sixth district of Nanyang, rushed to the scene to appease both sides, instructed them not to seek revenge again, and instructed local gentry to mediate the situation. This was in mid-October. However, Tian Ziyue was determined to avenge the death of his mother and younger brother, so he united with Zhao Zesan and others to seek help from Bie Tingfang. Bie sent six regiments of troops, who set out from Neixiang and went south. The journey of more than 140 li was reached in two days, directly approaching Dai Huanzhang's fifth district. However, Dai already had Zhang, Guo, Ding, and others to help him, and he had recently purchased more than 20 machine guns and hundreds of rifles from a certain division in Laohekou, and his strength had increased sixfold. He was unwilling to show weakness and resisted. As a result, the two sides were in constant artillery fire and fierce fighting until now. Now Dai's outnumbered troops have been broken in eight of the ten villages and are afraid that they will not be able to support them. Although Feng Jianfei has arrived at the scene, he can only mediate if he has no troops. It is said that he has telegraphed the provincial government to send a plane to help suppress the bandits. (27th Chat)

Page 11

The Government of Outer Mongolia Under Party Rule: The National Youth and National Parties Hold Power. All Systems Are the Same as Russian Organizations. 91

— Jin

Beijing Correspondence: The issue of Inner Mongolia's autonomy has come to an end after Huang Shaohong and Prince De and others met. However, the outside world knows little about the party and political situation in Outer Mongolia since its independence. Outer Mongolia and Inner Mongolia were originally one body. In the ninth year of the Republic of China, the Beijing government sent Xu Shuzheng, the Northwest Frontier Commissioner, to govern Outer Mongolia, mobilizing a large number of troops and carrying new weapons to Kulun to declare its goodwill towards Mongolia. Due to improper handling, the Kulun civil unrest broke out in the tenth year of the Republic of China. Since the fall of Outer Mongolia, internal strife has occurred frequently in our country, and few people have paid attention to the Mongolian issue. This year, Prince De advocated a high degree of autonomy in Bailing Temple. Although the central government sent senior officials to negotiate, it still did not pay attention to the actual situation in Outer Mongolia. Because Outer Mongolia and Inner Mongolia are connected, it is necessary to prevent infection. According to Ms. Wu Ling, a Mongolian who recently returned to Beijing from Kulun, the actual situation in Outer Mongolia is briefly recorded as follows:

(Process of Becoming Communist) The Mongolian people have been subject to the late Qing Dynasty for more than two hundred years. During these two hundred years, the foolishness suffered by the Mongolian people cannot be fully described. For this reason, there was the result of declaring independence from the late Qing Dynasty in 1911. Although the Mongolian people declared independence, they ultimately failed to succeed immediately due to their weak strength. Many twists and turns occurred in the middle, until 1920, when patriots organized the Outer Mongolian National Revolutionary Party and established the Mongolian National Revolutionary Government in the Tuylgolovsakhsk region. In March 1921, it issued a declaration and its outline for nation-building, which did not contain any communist color. On September 20 of the same year, about two months after Kulun was acquired, the government formulated the election law for the Small National Assembly. On October 27, the Small National Assembly opened, and although only 25 people attended, it occupied an important page in Mongolian history. At that time, it passed the government's proposed policy of freedom and democracy, abolished old laws, and formulated new laws and other important matters. However, the Mongolian Republic, with the assistance of the Soviet Union, adopted a constitutional system of European and American democracy, which was of course dissatisfied with by the Soviet Union and a group of Mongolian youth who returned from Russia, as well as dissatisfied members of the National Party. Therefore, a group of Mongolian youth who returned from Russia and dissatisfied members of the National Party, with the assistance of the Soviet Union, established the Mongolian Youth Revolutionary Party in Ulaanbaatar (Kulun) in August 1921. When it was first established, it was a small organization within the National Party, declaring its support for the National Party, and using the method of crossing party lines to mix with the National Party's work and supervise the government's left-leaning policies. Therefore, between the spring of 1922 and the autumn of 1923, the National Party split. As a result, the Youth Party won, and at the same time, the actual power of the government had to fall into the hands of the Youth Party. Therefore, the country's policy direction also changed at the same time. After the Youth Party won, the National Party's policies also became increasingly left-leaning. On July 8, 1924, the Mongolian government designated this day as a major memorial day, which coincided with the third anniversary of the expulsion of Wengeen from Ulaanbaatar, and on that day issued a declaration to implement the Soviet-style republican system. In November of the same year, it convened the Great National Assembly, passed the Declaration of the Rights of the Mongolian Laboring People, and formulated and promulgated the Constitution. At the same time, the representative of the International Communist Party sent a telegram to congratulate the conference, stating that the formulation of this Constitution was a major step forward in the Mongolian people's revolution and a success in the Eastern peoples' revolutionary movement. As a result, the Mongolian people stepped onto the stage of a communist society.

(Content of the Two Parties) The organization of the National Party adopts a committee system, with a Central Executive Committee located in Ulaanbaatar City to participate in national affairs, and branches are set up in various places to supervise the implementation of politics. The Central Executive Committee holds a general meeting of all representatives once a year to discuss various important issues within the party and related to politics. The organization of the Youth Party is not much different from that of the National Party. It also holds a general meeting of all party members once a year to report on the status of the year and discuss future plans. At the same time, it also elects 25 people as members of the Central Executive Committee. The Executive Committee meets twice a year to discuss methods for carrying out planned matters and elect a chairman. The Central Party Headquarters has an Organization Department to guide the organization and conduct of party affairs in various places, and a Propaganda Department to edit and publish various propaganda materials. Although the National Party and the Youth Party have formed an opposition in terms of organization, since the Youth Party gained power in 1924, the National Party's policies have also changed. Since the major purge within the party in 1925, it has become a purely red organization. Lin Di, the most powerful leader of the National Party, stated the following about the nature of the Mongolian Revolutionary Party in his paper "The Future of the Mongolian Revolution": "The ultimate goal of the Mongolian National Party is to realize communism." From this declaration, it can be seen that the National Party, which initially had the ideal of realizing constitutional politics, has in reality become a bubble. Therefore, although the two parties seem to be opposed on the surface, they are actually one. Moreover, the Youth Party is still a candidate for the National Party. Party members must be young people under the age of 25, and those who fight with the National Party are not separate factions, but only lead the National Party to the left.

(Political Organization) The Constitution of the Mongolian Republic was created by the Great National Assembly after the purpose of the National Party changed, so it is roughly the same as the Soviet Constitution. Therefore, the political organization is of course also similar. The organization of the Mongolian Republic is recorded as follows: (1) The highest power agency of the Mongolian Republic is the Great National Assembly. The Great National Assembly is organized by representatives elected from the people of villages and cities and the army. As for the number of members of the parliament, it is determined according to the population ratio of the electoral districts. The regular meeting of the Great National Assembly is convened by the Small National Assembly at least once a year. As for the temporary Great National Assembly, it is convened at the request of the Small National Assembly or more than one-third of the members of the Great National Assembly or more than one-third of the voters in the villages, similar to the Congress of Soviets of the Soviet Union. (2) During the adjournment of the Great National Assembly, the Small National Assembly becomes the organ that exercises the highest powers, that is, supervises the highest government organs, implements the resolutions of the Great National Assembly, and is responsible to the Great National Assembly, similar to the Central Executive Committee of the Soviet Union. The Small National Assembly is organized by members elected by the Great National Assembly. As for the convening period, it must be at least twice a year. (3) During the adjournment of the Small National Assembly, the highest legislative, executive, and command organ in the country is the Standing Committee of the Small National Assembly (i.e., the Cadre Council) and the State Council of the government, which is formed by members elected at each convening of the Small National Assembly. (4) The People's Committee is responsible for general state affairs, and its main power is in execution and command, but its highest legislative power is organized into: 1. Chairman of the People's Committee, 2. Vice Chairman of the People's Committee, 3. Chairman of the Military People's Committee, 4. Chairman of the Economic People's Committee, 5. Minister of the Internal Affairs People's Committee, 6. Minister of the Foreign Affairs People's Committee, 7. Minister of the Military People's Committee, 8. Minister of the Finance People's Committee, 9. Minister of the Justice People's Committee, 10. Minister of the Education People's Committee, 11. Minister of the Agriculture and Commerce People's Committee, 12. President of the Review Court, 13. Chief of the General Staff. In addition, there are two organs: 1. The Internal Investigation Office, 2. The Academy of Sciences. The Internal Investigation Office, also known as the National Government Security Bureau, is subordinate to the highest sovereignty and has absolute independent privileges, not subject to the interference of any other organ, and has three executive powers: the military police, the judiciary, and the police. It detects the entry and exit of travelers, prevents and controls the movement of residents, and arrests and imposes severe penalties on those who are suspected of being rebellious, so it is very similar to the Federal Political Security Bureau of the Soviet Union, and its purpose is nothing more than to prevent the occurrence of internal strife. The Academy of Sciences, also known as the National Academy of Sciences, is divided into the Library Department, the Museum Department, the Drawing Department, and the Compilation Department. It specializes in collecting ancient books and documents unique to Mongolia, as well as various products or academic reference materials, and specializes in translating new Mongolian books, surveying and mapping various maps, and teaching maps. Since its establishment, it has made considerable achievements in promoting the new and old cultural undertakings of Mongolia.

(Party-Government Relations) The Central Executive Committees of the Mongolian National Party and the Youth Party can be said to be the highest organs of the Mongolian government, standing behind the government and the parliament and holding real power, which is the same as the Communist Party of the Soviet Union standing behind the Soviet government and holding real power. Therefore, although the government's administrative policy is determined by the parliament, all bills of the parliament must be discussed and passed by the party before they can be handed over to the party group in the parliament. Moreover, all major political and economic matters concerning domestic and foreign affairs, as well as major issues that arise temporarily, must be discussed and decided by the party. Even matters decided by the State Council have the right to be rejected by the party, and the government only implements everything under the guidance of the party. In short, its relationship is "the party is the leader, and the government is the led", so it can be said to be "ruling the country with the party", that is, the dictatorship of the proletariat. The ultimate goal of the Mongolian National Party and the Youth Party is to realize a communist society, and at the same time, they represent the proletariat of Outer Mongolia today, so they are not similar to capitalist parties, which only represent the interests of individuals or a few people, but represent the interests of a class, in other words, they represent the interests of the majority. (28th)

Establishment of a Garrison Command in the Border Area of Jiangxi, Zhejiang, Fujian, and Anhui Zhao Guantao is the Garrison Commander. 92

Nanchang Correspondence: In order to consolidate the security of the border area of Jiangxi, Zhejiang, Fujian, and Anhui, and to increase the efficiency of bandit suppression, the Nanchang Military Camp has specially established a Garrison Command in the border area of Jiangxi, Zhejiang, Fujian, and Anhui, which will command the bandit suppression troops in the area, rectify discipline, and supervise the party and government organs to strictly enforce the cleaning operation. Zhao Shuotao was appointed as the garrison commander, and the organization regulations of the department were drafted and promulgated. Yesterday, it was ordered that all party, government, military, and police organs should transfer the order to their subordinates for unified knowledge. The organization regulations of the Garrison Command in the border area of Jiangxi, Zhejiang, Fujian, and Anhui are as follows:

Article 1: The Nanchang Military Camp of the Chairman of the Military Commission of the National Government, in order to consolidate the security of the border area of Jiangxi, Zhejiang, Fujian, and Anhui, and to unify the command of the bandit suppression troops in the area, rectify discipline, and supervise the party and government organs in the area to strictly enforce various joint suppression and cleaning operations, has specially established the Garrison Command in the border area of Jiangxi, Zhejiang, Fujian, and Anhui to handle it. Article 2: The Garrison Command in the border area of Jiangxi, Zhejiang, Fujian, and Anhui shall have one commander, who shall be concurrently appointed by the chairman from among the senior officers of the bandit suppression troops in the area, and shall be directly under the Nanchang Military Camp and under the command of the Commander-in-Chief of the Northern Route Army, and shall exercise his powers in the garrison area under his jurisdiction. Article 3: The garrison area under the jurisdiction of the garrison commander shall be temporarily determined as the northeastern part of Jiangxi and the counties in the border area of Zhejiang, Fujian, and Anhui adjacent to eastern Jiangxi, and shall be designated by the Nanchang Military Camp. Article 4: The garrison commander shall have the power to command and dispatch troops in the area under his jurisdiction, and the exercise of other garrison powers in the area under his jurisdiction shall be as follows: (1) Matters concerning guarding and defense, (1) Matters concerning the construction of bunkers and the development of transportation, (1) Matters concerning the repair of roads and bridges, Matters concerning the repair and defense of city defenses, (1) Matters concerning the review and spot check of household registration, (1) Matters concerning patrol and inspection, (1) Matters concerning the suppression and placement of vagrant soldiers and miscellaneous soldiers, (1) Matters concerning the handling of the transportation of wounded soldiers of various units, (1) Matters concerning fire protection, (1) Matters concerning the supervision and guidance of the organization and training of teams and the people (1) Matters concerning the inspection of vehicles, ships, travelers, (1) Matters concerning the protection of airports, military stations, warehouses, highway stations, communication equipment, and water and land terminals, (1) Matters concerning the punishment of endangering public safety and disturbing order, (1) Matters concerning the inspection and suppression of gatherings, associations, posts and telecommunications, and news, books, slogans, dramas, and all printed materials, (1) Matters concerning the temporary prohibition of the export of privately owned goods for military use, (1) Matters concerning the protection of harvesting and the blockade of bandit areas, (1) Matters concerning the inspection of homes and all buildings when necessary. Article 5: In addition to the provisions of the preceding article, the Garrison Command may also apply the provisions of Articles 3 and 4 of the Provisional Regulations for the Handling of Local Party and Government Affairs by the Commanders-in-Chief of the Northern Route Army in handling local party and government affairs in the area under its jurisdiction. Article 6: For the convenience of the garrison, the area under its jurisdiction may be divided into several garrison sub-areas, each with a number, and each sub-area shall have a commander to perform its duties. The commanders of each sub-area shall be appointed by the Nanchang Military Camp upon request of the garrison commander. Article 7: Banditry cases may be interrogated and sentenced by the Garrison Command, and submitted to the Nanchang Military Camp or the Headquarters of the Commander-in-Chief of the Northern Route Army for approval and implementation. Article 8: The inspection and patrol methods shall be in accordance with the regulations of the inspection and patrol rules of the Yongfeng, Nancheng, Fuzhou, and Xingan Garrison Commands. Article 9: The Garrison Command shall not set up a separate establishment, and all its tasks shall be handled concurrently by the officers and staff of the original troops of the concurrent commander. However, it shall be subsidized with the necessary office expenses every month, and the amount shall be determined separately by the military camp. Article 10: This regulation may be amended at any time if there are any matters not covered herein. Article 11: This regulation shall be implemented from the date of its promulgation. (November 29th, Datong News Agency)

Guangdong Province Handles Winter Defense, Orders the Guard Brigade to Return to the Provincial Capital, Land Defense in the Urban Area Starts on the 26th, and Winter Defense on All Rivers is Also Arranged in Detail. 93

Guangzhou Correspondence: Due to the recent changes in the situation, the military and police authorities have decided to organize winter defense starting from November 26 in order to protect public security. The Guangzhou Urban Area Guard Affairs will be the responsibility of the Kehui Public Security Bureau in conjunction with the Military Police Command, and the Guard Brigade, Chen Hanguang's troops, stationed in the Southern Route, will be ordered to return to the province to be responsible for the suburban guard. Chen's brigade has been ordered and can first draw a part of the troops to the province within a few days. The time for the implementation of winter defense in the urban area is from the 26th to the end of February next year. If necessary, the period may be extended. The winter defense measures are generally based on last year's regulations and have been modified appropriately. The main matters are to strictly inspect travelers in the urban area, send more secret agents to prevent gangsters from mixing in, organize armed patrol teams and bicycle patrol teams to patrol the city day and night, and the water police bureau will send patrol boats to patrol day and night, cracking down on lodging boats on the embankment. All public entertainment venues and hotels will be searched by detectives in rotation. All armed police officers in the public security sub-bureaus and the water police bureau in the urban area must be stationed in the bureau at all times, waiting for orders to be dispatched at any time. On the sea defense front, the authorities regard Humen as a coastal fortress, and it is urgent to send ships to station in sections inside and outside Humen and in the Pearl River basin. Therefore, Li Jiezhi, the commander of the Humen Fortress, returned to Humen on the 21st to arrange everything. Zhang Zhiying, the commander of the fleet, also took a ship to the Shi Tou River area in Henan Province to inspect the various sections of the fleet a few days ago. Because the river channel in the Sanshan Shibian area downstream of Nanshi Tou is the exit of the provincial river, the Jiangda warship was previously sent to station there to guard the key point. After Zhang's inspection, he ordered the Haikang warship to patrol the river surface there, and if any suspicious ships are found, they must be ordered to stop and be allowed to pass only after being inspected. The fleet headquarters also handles the winter defense and segment ship liaison in the east and west rivers in accordance with the precedents of last year. The Haihu warship was sent as the general patrol ship of the West River, and the Jianru warship was sent as the general patrol ship of the East River. As for the allocation of segment ships, the provincial river area, such as Dasha Tou, South Bank, Yadu Guan, Bai E Tan, Nan Shi Tou, and other river surfaces, are stationed with Zhongkai, Suijiang, Leiqian, Jinma, and Jiangping ships. The Zhixin warship patrols from Humen to Lianhua Mountain, and the Bao Bi warship patrols from Lingdingyang to Humen. In the lower reaches of the West River, Jiangda, Jianggong, and Jianghan are stationed from Nanhai Sanshan to Shunde Caoxie Zhou, the Kelu ship is stationed at Ying Ge Zui, the Beijiang ship is stationed at Sixianxi, and the Zhuiyun ship is stationed at Sanshui River Mouth. From Sanshui along the West River up to Guangli, Yuecheng, and Ducheng, there are Leigen, Leikan, Leilong, and Haiying ships stationed at each section. The Shilong and Xintang waterways in the East River are responsible for the blocking and stationing of the Fubo, Longxiang, and Haiou ships. (November 27th)

He Jingwu Rectifies the Pinghan Railway: Purchasing and Replacing Sleepers, Repairing Bridges, and Reducing the Travel Time of Express Trains 94

Hankou correspondence: Before the eighth year of the Republic (1919), the Pinghan Railway was known to be in good condition. However, after years of military destruction, its infrastructure deteriorated, leading to complaints from travelers and difficulties for merchants. Furthermore, the successive directors each held office for only a short time, lacking the opportunity to remedy the situation. In the past year, under the leadership of Commissioner He Jingwu, earnest efforts at rectification have been made. Over ten thousand steel rails and steel sleepers, and over five hundred thousand wooden sleepers, have been purchased and replaced. In addition, over twenty bridges, one hundred forty locomotives, and seven thousand freight cars have been repaired. Other facilities at various stations, such as platforms, shelters, fences, and overpasses, have also been repaired in succession. The railway now has a completely new look, washing away the sluggish atmosphere of the past. The express trains, regular express trains, and trains on various sections have also been well-equipped and run on schedule, providing convenience for passengers and merchants. In particular, the travel time of express trains, which previously took forty-eight hours from Hankou to Beiping, has now been reduced to thirty-nine hours. It is expected that the railway will soon be restored to its original condition before the eighth year of the Republic.

The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance Dispatches Personnel to Clean Up Xuzhou Paper Money: Thoroughly Eliminating and Preventing the Issuance of Private Currency, Over 50,000 Yuan of Paper Money Has Already Been Burned 95

The private paper money crisis in Xuzhou has lasted for a relatively long time and is gradually showing signs of easing. However, a thorough solution has yet to be heard. Public exchange offices and various ticket shops still limit self-exchange to one yuan. The exchange places are crowded with people every day, and injuries are not uncommon. The Provincial Department of Finance has specially dispatched Commissioner Wu Gengyu to Xuzhou to supervise the cleanup. Wu has taken up residence at the Garden Hotel and initially engaged in investigative work, followed by consultations with party and government authorities and various sectors regarding cleanup strategies. Today (29th), Wu held another round of discussions at the Garden Hotel with responsible personnel from the party, government, and chambers of commerce, and progress seems to be gradually emerging. Mr. Wu also told reporters that he was sent to Xuzhou based on the intentions of the provincial department and the demands of the people of Xuzhou, determined to thoroughly eliminate the issuance of private currency. After investigating in Xuzhou, he felt that the ticket amounts reported by the various ticket shops should be further secured with guarantees, and the declared assets should also be publicly appraised to avoid the abuses of exaggeration and concealment, in order to provide a sufficient basis for the cleanup. Yesterday, the various ticket shops completed the guarantee procedures for the ticket amounts, and the assets are currently being appraised. This valuation must be estimated at the lowest possible value to avoid future disputes. It is planned that after the valuation procedures are completed, a financial adjustment committee will be organized by local impartial individuals to manage the assets and issue bonds to recover the existing private tickets. The number of these bonds will be limited to the amount of private tickets to be recovered. After the assets are auctioned, the bonds will be gradually recovered and destroyed. This method is considered more reliable, and both the current maintenance and future cleanup can be resolved from this. However, the issuance of bonds must have a fund to support the exchange, which requires cash. Therefore, this method has two major difficulties: first, whether the assets of each company can offset the ticket amount is a concern; second, the bond fund is currently difficult to raise. These issues still need to be gradually addressed. In addition, among the seven private ticket shops, Gongyu is a public-share company with many shareholders who have assets. She Yingchang has ordered the shareholders to clean up on their own and make as much redemption as possible, and a solution may be reached within days. If Gongyu can resolve its own situation and remove its 140,000 yuan ticket amount, it will reduce the difficulty of handling the remaining tickets. This plan is expected to be finalized in about a week, and efforts are currently underway towards this goal. As for the cleanup committee established by the county government, it has already implemented its resolution to burn the tickets yesterday. In the afternoon of yesterday (28th), the original tickets stored by each ticket shop and the tickets redeemed in recent days, totaling 253,075 strings and 500 cash, were burned in front of the county government's auditorium. Provincial Commissioner Wu Gengyu and representatives from various sectors were present to supervise. First, County Magistrate She Nianci reported the severity of the paper money disaster in Xuzhou, now facing the verge of collapse, determined to thoroughly clean up and eliminate the ticket scourge. Then, Commissioner Wu randomly checked the amounts, which were consistent. The amounts of each ticket shop were: Chunquan 27,880 strings and 500 cash, Yizhenxiang 10,000 strings, Buxinji 28,500 strings, Juhe 1,800 strings, Tianbaoyu 52,450 strings, Shixingchang 16,445 strings, Gongyu 116,000 strings. The ticket bundles were unpacked and scattered in the courtyard, then ignited with sorghum stalks and kerosene. The piles of paper money were completely consumed by the fire. It was found that the total ticket amount was 420,000 yuan, and this was the first burning, destroying 50,000 yuan, equivalent to one-eighth of the total. The remaining 300,000 yuan are still being squeezed out and awaiting redemption. (November 29th)

Wuxi: The County Government Issues an Arrest Warrant for Xi Huian 99

The Tonghui Road Huisheng Silk Factory suffered losses and went bankrupt, and the manager, Xi Huian, fled without a trace. The factory's male and female workers have not been paid for two months, causing a major uproar. The workers gradually gathered more than a hundred people and went to the Huichang Silk Factory in Nanqiao, demanding that all shares under Xi Huian's name in the factory be withdrawn as compensation. They refused to leave. Yesterday morning, the county government invited the county party headquarters, the county chamber of commerce, the silk factory guild, and the Huichang manager Shou Yiting to jointly discuss the matter and decided as follows: (1) All shares under Xi Huian's name in the Huichang Silk Factory, actually paid up to 1,500 yuan, will be withdrawn immediately. From now on, Huichang will sever ties with Xi Huian. Huichang Factory will still seek compensation from Xi Huian for the various losses suffered by Huichang due to Xi Huian. (2) The workers of Huisheng will be ordered by the party and government to leave Huichang immediately and express their apologies to Huichang. (3) Xi Huian has fled without a trace, owing wages to the workers and affecting social security. The county government will issue an arrest warrant and order him to be brought to justice and ordered to clean up. After the above methods were discussed and decided, the remaining wages will be raised by the Chamber of Commerce Industry Association from the Ruichang Run Silver Bank, which received the spring and summer dry cocoons of Huisheng, and the new wealth added by Huisheng. It is allowed to pay all the arrears of wages today.

Changshu: A Fifty-One-Year-Old Woman Commits Adultery and Murders Her Husband 105

Chen Jintang, a cook in Zhangjiashi in the tenth district of this county, is currently fifty years old. On the 25th of this month, he was suddenly murdered by his wife, Wang, who is fifty-one years old. This is because she is passionately in love with another man, which led her to commit this heinous act. This has attracted considerable attention in society. After the district chief reported to the county, Judge Guo, accompanied by the coroner and a Western doctor, went to the countryside on the 28th to conduct an examination. According to Chen Xiaohuai, the deceased's son, who is nineteen years old, his father was a cook. Because of his skillful cooking, he was known as a famous chef by the villagers. On the night of the 25th of this month, he returned from cooking at the house of his uncle Chen Xingjia. His mother immediately urged him to eat. However, his parents had been married for more than thirty years and often quarreled, so they were almost like strangers. Although my mother is over forty years old, she is openly cohabiting with Lin San nearby. However, when he returned that night, his mother suddenly changed her usual behavior and served him diligently. Jintang could not bear to disobey her, so he ate. Unexpectedly, he felt severe abdominal pain after the meal. Everyone suspected that it was a sudden illness and planned to call a doctor. Wang refused, saying that it would be cured in a moment and that everyone could sleep peacefully. Unexpectedly, after a while, they suddenly heard a cry for help. They rushed to check and saw that Tang Jin was lying on the bed. His brother, Jinsheng, kept a watch on the murderer. At dawn, he sent her to the police station and reported to the county for examination. When Judge Guo arrived in the countryside, he ordered the arrest of the adulterer Lin San, who had already disappeared. The examination revealed that the body's abdomen was now green and black, and there were heavy finger marks on the neck, indicating that he had been poisoned and strangled to death before death. However, what poison he had taken is still under investigation. He ordered the corpse's family to coffin him on their own. As for the murderer, Chen Wang, she was escorted to the Ninth Police Station and detained. That night, during dinner, while the guard, Gu Shiliang, was eating, Wang escaped through the window. Wang Zhihuai, the patrol officer of the station, submitted a report to the bureau requesting punishment and reported the above information to Judge Guo. Guo believed that such a serious murderer should not be allowed to escape, so he ordered that the case be handed over within five days. The guard, Gu Shiliang, is suspected of negligence and has been ordered to submit a written guarantee of 5,000 yuan. The Public Security Bureau has now issued a notice to various villages, offering a reward for her arrest.

Nantong: County Police Team Arrests Kidnappers 106

The Nantong County Police Team arrested three well-known kidnappers, Lu Xiwu, Bai Changli, and Chen Wanglian, in the west of the city. Li Liejun Issues Original Letter to Chairman Jiang, Calling for the Liberation of People's Freedoms of Speech and Publication as the Fundamental Key to Domestic Security and Foreign Defense 109

Xin Xin News Agency reports: Member of the Central Committee Li Liejun previously sent a letter to Chairman of the Military Commission Jiang Jieshi, making suggestions on the handling of the Fujian incident and the opening up of political power. To this end, Mr. Li issued a written statement the day before yesterday morning, and yesterday morning he re-issued the original letter to Mr. Jiang. It is recorded as follows: "I have been in Kuangshan for a long time, and several months have passed. I hope that you are in good health and that my distant blessings are in line. Vulgar words are always valued as rare, so I have not reported in writing for a long time. Now Fujian has declared independence again. Although the outcome of the matter is unknown (omitted), I am deeply afraid of the country's danger and the public's confusion, so I cannot help but hope that at this time, the way to save and relieve the situation is to quickly liberate the people's freedoms of speech, publication, assembly, and association, and to grant them equal treatment in law and politics. This is the fundamental key to gathering wisdom and energy, securing the country internally, and defending against foreign aggression. All of this is what you, sir, have agreed to in the past, and now its implementation is even more evident. Otherwise, when will the world be settled? From the beginning of the Fujian incident, a peaceful solution should have a way, which lies in making good decisions. I respectfully offer a few words, and I hope that you, sir, will consider them."

Rumors in the City that the Min Army Struck First, with Reports of Contact on the Fujian-Zhejiang Border 110

Since the Fujian rebellion, the central government initially intended to resolve it through political means. However, due to the Fujian province's actions of spying on Zhejiang, it was decided to use military sanctions. Therefore, in recent days, a large army has been mobilized and concentrated in Xianxia, Yandang, and other places, preparing to issue an order to suppress the rebellion. Unexpectedly, the military authorities of Fujian province are planning to strike first. According to news from the transportation sector yesterday, Xin Sheng News Agency reported that it was widely rumored in Shanghai yesterday that contact had begun in the Xianxia area on the Fujian-Zhejiang border. After Xin Sheng News Agency reporters inquired, they learned that the central army is currently taking a defensive position and has not ordered an attack. However, the rumor of contact is also possible. After the establishment of the Fujian Provincial People's Government, it has been criticized by various parties and is in a lonely situation. It does need to seek outward development urgently in order to strike first and seek a way out. A certain member of the Central Committee expressed regret over the rumors of contact on the Fujian-Zhejiang border, because the outbreak of war would have a significant impact on the autumn harvest. At a time when the rural economy is on the verge of bankruptcy, the farmers in the area, who have worked hard for years, are once again in despair.

Maps claim that the Min army is about to reach Pingyang, Ruian, and other places in Zhejiang Province to spy on Wenzhou. However, the central army has already stationed a considerable number of troops in that area. Therefore, if the Min army advances again, formal contact will inevitably occur. According to a person who arrived in Shanghai on the Sanjiang steamer from Pingyang on the 25th of this month, when he left Pingyang, the central army was gathering there, with a sense of imminent eruption. Therefore, the local finance has fallen into a state of chaos, and merchants have stopped loading passengers and goods, and the market is depressed, even to the point of complete stagnation.

More than ten people from the New Voice Society report that Liu Heding and Zhou Zhiqin's troops in northern Fujian are adjacent to the defense area of the 19th Route Army. The 19th Route Army, believing that Liu and Zhou were determined to support the central government and unwilling to cooperate at all, planned to exert pressure on Liu and Zhou, and searched their offices in the provincial capital. Tao Yungu, director of Liu's office, and Hu Xingqiao, director of Zhou's office, were well prepared in advance, so they managed to escape with difficulty, but the loss of equipment and luggage was considerable. Now, Tao Yungu, Hu Xingqiao, Li Dingzhang (former Fuzhou garrison commander) of Liu's army, and more than ten others arrived in Shanghai yesterday. Upon hearing the news, reporters from the New Voice Society rushed to visit them at their hotel. According to their account, the situation in Fujian is as follows:

Complexity of the Fujian Situation: The complexity of the situation in Fujian this time can be said to have reached its peak. The Fujian side has gathered all those who are not tolerated by all parties. Our troops have been stationed in the northern Fujian area and have been on good terms with the local people. Since the arrival of the 19th Route Army in Fujian, we have gained even more support from the people in comparison, because the measures taken by the 19th Route Army in Fujian have not been well received by the people of Fujian. Moreover, our troops have been in Fujian for many years and are more familiar with the situation, so the Fujian side has tried to win us over in various ways, and tempted us with various benefits.

Rejection of Representatives: Before the Fujian Incident, Chen Mingshu sent many people to our troops to meet with our superiors, but to no avail. When rumors were rife on the 18th, Chen and Cai sent Division Commander Deng Shizeng again, intending to meet with our division and brigade commanders to seek a final solution. Our division and brigade commanders still refused by telegram, which caused them to become angry.

Support for the Central Government: The final intention of the Fujian side has also been expressed many times, saying that if our two troops can earnestly participate, they will be specially expanded, and the funding will also be specially increased. If our two troops do not want to participate, then please strictly maintain neutrality, do not favor any side, and the province will continue to provide assistance as usual. However, our troops are still determined to ignore them, uphold the intention of supporting the central government, and persevere to the end.

Combat Capabilities: Now our division (Liu Heding's division) has concentrated in the Jian'ou area from Yanping, and our brigade (Zhou Zhiqin's brigade) is still stationed in Shaowu and other places, and the original defense has not moved. Chairman Chiang has already sent a telegram instructing us to await further orders, and there should be no movement for the time being. Moreover, after the 19th Route Army arrived in Fujian, they have gained a very detailed understanding of the combat capabilities of our two troops in the successive bandit suppression campaigns. Without sufficient preparation, they will not rashly attack.

Entering Beijing and Transferring to Jiangxi: We had previously received a telegram from our superiors, determined to support the central government, so we had made preparations early. All subordinate personnel have been secretly dismissed, but equipment and luggage, heavy objects, cannot be moved, and are still sealed up. The losses are considerable. We received a telegram from our superiors on the 25th and immediately left the province secretly. After various difficulties, we arrived in Shanghai today. We now plan to rest for a while, enter Beijing and transfer to Jiangxi, and report the details, because our superiors have already sent a telegram instructing us to report everything to the relevant authorities.

Naval Battalion Commander Chen: According to the China News Agency, after Rong Yinglin, the fortress commander appointed by the Fujian side, took over Mawei, all the heads of naval departments in Fujian have fled separately. Only Chen Tianjing, the commander of the Mawei Training Camp of the Navy Department, escaped from Fujian and arrived in Shanghai yesterday. Regular Collection of Land Value Tax in the Two Districts of Shanghai South and Zhabei; Announcement Issued Yesterday by the Municipal Finance Bureau; Limited to Two Months Starting from the 21st 115

According to the Central News Agency, the matter of collecting land value tax in this city, regarding the land in areas one to seven in the South Shanghai District and areas one and two in the Zhabei District, has been determined for land value by the Land Valuation Committee. The Municipal Finance Bureau has received an order from the Municipal Government approving the collection of five-sixths of the land value tax for the second half of this year in all areas where the land value has been determined. It is scheduled to begin collecting taxes on the 21st of this month. The municipal announcement is recorded below: It has been investigated that the regulations for the temporary collection of land value tax in this city, as well as the scope of collection and the start date of collection, have been announced and implemented by the Municipal Government successively. Now, the land in areas one to seven in the South Shanghai District and areas one and two in the Zhabei District have been valued by the Land Valuation Committee, and submitted by the Land Bureau together with this bureau to the Municipal Government for approval and announcement. All land in the above-mentioned areas that has been valued shall pay five-sixths of the second installment of the land value tax for this year. It is hereby decided to start collecting taxes on December 21st of this year, and the deadline for payment is two months from the start date, ending on February 20th of the 23rd year. Those whose land is in the South Shanghai District shall pay at the South Shanghai Tax Collection Office of this bureau in Maojia Lane, Nanshi, and those in the Zhabei District shall pay at the North Shanghai Tax Collection Office of this bureau on Datong Road, Zhabei. Those who fail to pay within the deadline will be pursued in accordance with Article 8 of the Provisional Regulations for the Collection of Land Value Tax and Article 23 of the Implementing Rules, and annual interest will be added to the amount owed, and the income from the land will be extracted and auctioned off in proportion to the number of years in arrears in order to comply with the regulations. In addition to sending the notices separately, this announcement is hereby issued to all taxpayers to abide by and pay within the deadline, without delay, lest they be punished. If the notices have not yet been received, they should state their current address or mailing address to the bureau within the deadline for verification and re-delivery, and should not delay themselves.
